## ЁЯУЦ Legend

### File Types
- ЁЯУД Other: Other files
- ЁЯУД Docs: Text files
- ЁЯУЦ Docs: Markdown files
- тЪЩя╕П Config: TOML files
- ЁЯЪл DevOps: Git ignore

### Importance Levels
- ЁЯФ┤ Critical: Essential project files
- ЁЯЯб High: Important configuration files
- ЁЯФ╡ Medium: Helpful but not essential files
